         by
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/author/pamhouseofhawthornes-com/" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Pam
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/#comments">
           49 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <p>
         I have really scaled back in what I am doing inside and out for fall decor this year. I dont know, but I think I sort of got burned out by being a new blogger last year.
        </p>
        <p>
         Back then I was all excited to do decorating for the seasons and sort of went all out. This year its much more laid back. And honestly, anything that I put out for fall will have to be put away again and that in itself is a drawback to me.
        </p>
        <p>
         So I just added a few key fall items to my summer porch and called it a day.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7683.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7683.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7683-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <a name="more">
         </a>
         <br/>
         The planters on either side of the door are what I had planted in May. They each have two Electric Lime Coleus with one Purple Fountain Grass plant in the middle. Sort of like a grass sandwich. But you dont have to eat it.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7634.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7634.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7634-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <span id="more-461">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         Gourds that I picked up at the farm market are sitting in my planter box along with a lid to an apple basket.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7666.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7666.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7666-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         Normally, I am not a fan of warty things, but I just love these bumpy gourds.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7667.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7667.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7667-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         The rocking chairs and pillows have stayed the same.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7678.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7678.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7678-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         I have added the clay pumpkin. Because, of course, I didnt have that out all summer. That would just be silly.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7626.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7626.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7626-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         The cornstalks were a huge splurge this year. I have a hard time spending money on something that I could just as easily grab from a nearby cornfield. I mean there are probably 14 bazillion cornstalks in a square mile radius of us. But that would be stealing. So I bought them at the farm market for $5.95 per stalk.
        </p>
        <p>
         I really do love the look of the cornstalks on the porch pillars though.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7641.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7641.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7641-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         I added a mum in an apple basket to the porch for a shot of fall color
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7685.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7685.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7685-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         along with my vintage 1950s Structo dump truck.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7671.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7671.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7671-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         The scale of the pumpkins is a little too large for this truck, but youll just have to imagine they were grown at the nuclear power plant.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7648.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7648.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7648-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         Hope you are enjoying your fall. Indian summer has hit Ohio and it should be a wonderful weekend to get out and enjoy the last of the warmth before the snow starts flying.
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7624.jpg">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7624.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="480" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/IMG_7624-650x488.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/Fall-Front-Porch-11.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" border="0" class="pib-hover-img" data-pin-media="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/Fall-Front-Porch-11.jpg" data-pin-url="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/fall-front-porch-2011/" height="640" src="http://www.houseofhawthornes.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/10/Fall-Front-Porch-11.jpg" title="Fun fall front porch decor - from houseofhawthornes.com" width="246"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
        <center>
         <a data-pin-config="none" data-pin-do="buttonPin" data-pin-height="28" href="https://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.houseofhawthornes.com%2F2011%2F10%2Ffall-front-porch-2011.html&amp;media=http%3A%2F%2F3.bp.blogspot.com%2F-KEx-Zb_ZSgU%2FU-ZP-palrlI%2FAAAAAAAAdKU%2FjwHITiPU0EM%2Fs1600%2FFall%2BFront%2BPorch%2B11.jpg&amp;description=Fun%20fall%20front%20porch%20decor%20-%20from%20houseofhawthornes.com" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.houseofhawthornes.com%2F2011%2F10%2Ffall-front-porch-2011.html&amp;media=http%3A%2F%2F3.bp.blogspot.com%2F-KEx-Zb_ZSgU%2FU-ZP-palrlI%2FAAAAAAAAdKU%2FjwHITiPU0EM%2Fs1600%2FFall%2BFront%2BPorch%2B11.jpg&amp;description=Fun%20fall%20front%20porch%20decor%20-%20from%20houseofhawthornes.com', '');">

         </a>
         <br/>

        </center>
